\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ raylib\ v5.1-\/dev\ -\/\ A\ simple\ and\ easy-\/to-\/use\ library\ to\ enjoy\ videogames\ programming\ (www.raylib.com)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ FEATURES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ NO\ external\ dependencies,\ all\ required\ libraries\ included\ with\ raylib}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Multiplatform:\ Windows,\ Linux,\ FreeBSD,\ OpenBSD,\ NetBSD,\ DragonFly,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ MacOS,\ Haiku,\ Android,\ Raspberry\ Pi,\ DRM\ native,\ HTML5.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Written\ in\ plain\ C\ code\ (C99)\ in\ PascalCase/camelCase\ notation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Hardware\ accelerated\ with\ OpenGL\ (1.1,\ 2.1,\ 3.3,\ 4.3\ or\ ES2\ -\/\ choose\ at\ compile)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Unique\ OpenGL\ abstraction\ layer\ (usable\ as\ standalone\ module):\ [rlgl]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Multiple\ Fonts\ formats\ supported\ (TTF,\ XNA\ fonts,\ AngelCode\ fonts)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Outstanding\ texture\ formats\ support,\ including\ compressed\ formats\ (DXT,\ ETC,\ ASTC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Full\ 3d\ support\ for\ 3d\ Shapes,\ Models,\ Billboards,\ Heightmaps\ and\ more!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Flexible\ Materials\ system,\ supporting\ classic\ maps\ and\ PBR\ maps}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Animated\ 3D\ models\ supported\ (skeletal\ bones\ animation)\ (IQM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Shaders\ support,\ including\ Model\ shaders\ and\ Postprocessing\ shaders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Powerful\ math\ module\ for\ Vector,\ Matrix\ and\ Quaternion\ operations:\ [raymath]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Audio\ loading\ and\ playing\ with\ streaming\ support\ (WAV,\ OGG,\ MP3,\ FLAC,\ XM,\ MOD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ VR\ stereo\ rendering\ with\ configurable\ HMD\ device\ parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Bindings\ to\ multiple\ programming\ languages\ available!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ One\ default\ Font\ is\ loaded\ on\ InitWindow()-\/>LoadFontDefault()\ [core,\ text]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ One\ default\ Texture2D\ is\ loaded\ on\ rlglInit(),\ 1x1\ white\ pixel\ R8G8B8A8\ [rlgl]\ (OpenGL\ 3.3\ or\ ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ One\ default\ Shader\ is\ loaded\ on\ rlglInit()-\/>rlLoadShaderDefault()\ [rlgl]\ (OpenGL\ 3.3\ or\ ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ One\ default\ RenderBatch\ is\ loaded\ on\ rlglInit()-\/>rlLoadRenderBatch()\ [rlgl]\ (OpenGL\ 3.3\ or\ ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
